# SID's Marathon Master Schedule

**Marathon Name:** SID's Marathon

## Daily Timetable

### Cycle 4: Mathematical Foundations & Digital Design Basics (Days 1–7)

#### Cycle 4 — Day 1 — Monday

- **Domain:** ECE
  - **Theme:** Algebra, Logarithms & Matrix Foundations
- **Primary Topic:** UNIT I-II: Algebra (Logarithms, Partial Fractions) & Matrices and Determinants
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Logarithms: definition, properties, natural and common logarithms
  - Exponential functions and e (Euler's number)
  - Logarithm equations and inequalities
  - Partial fraction decomposition for complex expressions
  - Matrix algebra: addition, subtraction, multiplication
  - Determinants: calculation, properties, minors and cofactors
  - Inverse matrices and matrix equations
  - System of linear equations using matrices
  - Applications to circuit analysis and signal processing
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Matrix representations in hardware
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Vector and matrix operations in quantum mechanics
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Logarithmic scaling in sensor data
  - Cross-Link (Python): NumPy matrix operations
- **Learning Objective:** Master logarithmic functions, partial fractions, and matrix algebra for applications in engineering.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Theory / 30m Intuition / 40m Problem Solving / 20m Review (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Set of 5 Solved Problems (logarithm simplification, partial fractions, matrix operations, determinants, system of equations)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #mathematics #GATE

#### Cycle 4 — Day 2 — Tuesday

- **Domain:** VHDL
  - **Theme:** Digital Design Fundamentals & RTL Essentials
- **Primary Topic:** VHDL Basics: Entity, Architecture, Libraries, and Digital Abstraction
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Transistor to logic gate abstraction
  - VHDL design units: entity and architecture
  - Libraries and packages (IEEE, std_logic_1164)
  - Port definitions: input, output, inout
  - Data types: bit, std_logic, std_logic_vector
  - Concurrent vs sequential statements
  - Basic combinational logic (AND, OR, NOT, MUX)
  - Behavioral vs structural modeling
  - Testbench basics
  - Synthesis vs simulation
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Digital gate behavior and timing
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Quantum bit representation
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Digital I/O on microcontrollers
  - Cross-Link (Python): HDL simulation with Python testbenches
- **Learning Objective:** Understand VHDL fundamentals and write basic synthesizable designs.
- **Session Breakdown:** 40m Theory / 20m Intuition / 60m Coding / 30m Practice (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Working VHDL Code (AND/OR gate entity, 2-to-1 multiplexer, SR latch model)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #coding #VHDL #digital_design

#### Cycle 4 — Day 3 — Wednesday

- **Domain:** Quantum
  - **Theme:** Mathematical Foundations for Quantum Mechanics
- **Primary Topic:** Vector Spaces, Linear Operators, and Functional Analysis
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Vector space axioms and properties
  - Finite and infinite dimensional spaces
  - Linear independence and basis vectors
  - Inner product and orthogonality
  - Gram-Schmidt orthogonalization process
  - Linear operators and transformations
  - Matrix representation of operators
  - Eigenvalues and eigenvectors concept
  - Functional analysis basics
  - Normed and Hilbert spaces
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Signal vector representation
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Vector/matrix hardware representations
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Vector operations in firmware
  - Cross-Link (Python): NumPy vector operations and linear algebra
- **Learning Objective:** Build mathematical foundation for quantum mechanics through vector spaces and linear algebra.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Theory / 30m Intuition / 40m Problem Solving / 20m Review (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Set of 5 Solved Problems (vector space verification, basis transformation, orthogonalization, eigenvalue concepts)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #mathematics #quantum #linear_algebra

#### Cycle 4 — Day 4 — Thursday

- **Domain:** Embedded
  - **Theme:** Arduino Hardware Architecture & Microcontroller Basics
- **Primary Topic:** Arduino Platform, Microcontroller Fundamentals, Board Architecture
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Introduction to microcontrollers and embedded systems
  - Arduino ecosystem and board families (Uno, Mega, Due, Nano)
  - AVR and ARM microcontroller architectures
  - Pin configuration and GPIO basics
  - Power supply and voltage domains
  - Clock sources and timing
  - Memory organization: Flash, RAM, EEPROM
  - Bootloader and firmware upload
  - Arduino IDE and development environment
  - Serial communication basics (UART)
  - Interrupt basics and handling
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Digital electronics and circuits
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Hardware description analogies
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Quantum state measurement as IO
  - Cross-Link (Python): Arduino programming in C
- **Learning Objective:** Understand Arduino hardware architecture and microcontroller fundamentals for embedded system design.
- **Session Breakdown:** 40m Theory / 20m Intuition / 60m Coding / 30m Practice (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Working Code (LED blink sketch, button input reading, serial communication test)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #coding #Arduino #embedded

#### Cycle 4 — Day 5 — Friday

- **Domain:** ECE
  - **Theme:** Trigonometric Functions & Angular Relationships
- **Primary Topic:** UNIT III-IV: Trigonometry - Functions, Identities, Compound Angles
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Trigonometric ratios: sine, cosine, tangent, cotangent, secant, cosecant
  - Unit circle and radian measure
  - Trigonometric identities: Pythagorean, reciprocal, quotient
  - Allied angles and angle relationships
  - Compound angle formulas (addition, subtraction)
  - Multiple angle formulas
  - Product-to-sum and sum-to-product formulas
  - Inverse trigonometric functions
  - Applications to AC circuits, waves, and signals
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Signal generation and waveform modeling
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Wave functions and oscillations
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Sine/cosine calculations in firmware
  - Cross-Link (Python): NumPy trigonometric operations
- **Learning Objective:** Master trigonometric identities and angle relationships for signal processing and circuit analysis.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Theory / 30m Intuition / 40m Problem Solving / 20m Review (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Set of 5 Solved Problems (allied angles, compound angles, multiple angles, wave applications, transformations)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #trigonometry #signal_processing

#### Cycle 4 — Day 6 — Saturday

- **Domain:** Python
  - **Theme:** Programming Fundamentals & Core Language Concepts
- **Primary Topic:** Python Basics: Installation, Variables, Data Types, Operators
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Python history and design philosophy
  - Installation and environment setup
  - REPL (Read-Eval-Print Loop) basics
  - Variables and naming conventions
  - Data types: int, float, str, bool, None
  - Type conversion and checking
  - Arithmetic, comparison, logical operators
  - String operations and formatting
  - Comments and documentation
  - Input/output operations
  - Basic error handling
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Hardware representation of data types
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Quantum state representation
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Microcontroller data types
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Circuit parameter calculations
- **Learning Objective:** Establish foundational Python programming skills including syntax, data types, and basic operations.
- **Session Breakdown:** 40m Theory / 20m Intuition / 60m Coding / 30m Practice (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Working Code (variable manipulation, type conversions, arithmetic operations, input/output programs, calculator)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #coding #python #fundamentals

#### Cycle 4 — Day 7 — Sunday

- **Domain:** Revision
  - **Theme:** Integrated Learning - Cycle 4 Mastery
- **Primary Topic:** Cycle 4 Consolidation - Mathematical Foundations across All Domains
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - ECE review: logarithms, matrices, determinants, trigonometry foundations
  - VHDL review: entity-architecture pattern, basic combinational logic
  - Quantum review: vector spaces, linear operators, mathematical basis
  - Embedded review: Arduino architecture, GPIO, serial communication
  - Python review: data types, operators, basic IO
  - Cross-domain synthesis: mathematical foundations in all domains
  - Problem-solving integration: combining concepts
  - Self-assessment and gap identification
  - GATE/ECET exam preparation for foundational topics
  - Planning for next cycle advancement
- **Learning Objective:** Achieve mastery across all five domains with integrated problem-solving.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Review / 60m Problem Solving / 30m Integration & Reflection (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Complete Cycle 4 Assessment (10 integrated problems, system design document, reflection portfolio)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #review #mastery #integration

### Cycle 5: Inverse Trigonometry & VHDL Processes (Days 8–14)

#### Cycle 5 — Day 8 — Monday

- **Domain:** ECE
  - **Theme:** Inverse Trigonometry & Triangle Solutions
- **Primary Topic:** UNIT V-VI: Trigonometry III (Inverse Functions) & Applications of Trigonometry
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Inverse trigonometric functions: arcsin, arccos, arctan, arccot, arcsec, arccsc
  - Domain and range restrictions
  - Inverse function properties and identities
  - Principal values
  - Triangle solution methods: ASA, SAS, SSS cases
  - Law of sines and law of cosines
  - Area of triangles using trigonometry
  - Bearing and navigation problems
  - Height and distance calculations
  - Applications in surveying and engineering
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Angle calculations in digital systems
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Phase and angle operators
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Angle measurements from sensors
  - Cross-Link (Python): arcsin, arccos, arctan in NumPy
- **Learning Objective:** Master inverse trigonometric functions and apply triangle solution methods to real-world engineering problems.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Theory / 30m Intuition / 40m Problem Solving / 20m Review (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Set of 5 Solved Problems (inverse function calculations, triangle solutions, bearing problems, angle determinations)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #trigonometry #applications

#### Cycle 5 — Day 9 — Tuesday

- **Domain:** VHDL
  - **Theme:** Concurrency & Process Model
- **Primary Topic:** VHDL Concurrency, Processes, Signals vs Variables & Modeling Styles
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Concurrent statement execution in VHDL
  - Process declaration and sensitivity list
  - Sequential statements within processes
  - Signals: declaration, assignment, event-driven behavior
  - Variables: local scope, immediate assignment
  - Signal update and delta cycles
  - Clocked processes for sequential logic
  - Combinational vs sequential processes
  - Behavioral, dataflow, and structural modeling
  - Synthesis of different modeling styles
  - Testbench and simulation concepts
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Gate-level concurrency
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Quantum state evolution
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Concurrent task execution
  - Cross-Link (Python): Object-oriented parallel patterns
- **Learning Objective:** Understand VHDL concurrency model, process execution, and signal-variable differences.
- **Session Breakdown:** 40m Theory / 20m Intuition / 60m Coding / 30m Practice (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Working VHDL Code (4-to-1 multiplexer with concurrent/process styles, SR latch, combinational logic models)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #coding #VHDL #concurrency

#### Cycle 5 — Day 10 — Wednesday

- **Domain:** Quantum
  - **Theme:** Complex Analysis for Quantum Theory
- **Primary Topic:** Complex Analysis & Functions - Analyticity, Contour Integration, Residues
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Complex numbers: Cartesian and polar forms
  - Complex plane and Argand diagram
  - Analytic (holomorphic) functions
  - Cauchy-Riemann equations
  - Singularities: poles, essential, branch points
  - Laurent series expansion
  - Residue theorem and pole classification
  - Contour integration techniques
  - Residue calculation methods
  - Applications to real integral evaluation
  - Dispersion relations in physics
  - Cross-Link (ECE): AC circuit analysis with phasors
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Complex number arithmetic in hardware
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Complex signal processing
  - Cross-Link (Python): cmath module and SciPy functions
- **Learning Objective:** Master complex analysis techniques essential for quantum mechanics and wave physics.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Theory / 30m Intuition / 40m Problem Solving / 20m Review (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Set of 5 Solved Problems (analytic function verification, residue calculations, contour integrals, dispersion relations)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #complex_analysis #quantum

#### Cycle 5 — Day 11 — Thursday

- **Domain:** Embedded
  - **Theme:** Arduino C Programming Fundamentals
- **Primary Topic:** C Language Basics for Arduino - Variables, Control Structures, Functions
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Data types in Arduino C: byte, int, long, float, char, boolean
  - Variable declaration and scope
  - Constants and macros
  - Conditional statements: if, else if, else
  - Switch-case statements
  - Loops: for, while, do-while

#### Cycle 5 — Day 12 — Friday

#### Cycle 5 — Day 13 — Saturday

- **Primary Topic:** Python Data Structures - Lists, Tuples, Dictionaries, Sets
- **Subtopics to cover:**

  - Nested data structures
  - Memory efficiency considerations

### Cycle 6: Units, Dimensions & VHDL Types/Packages (Days 15–21)

  - Dimensional homogeneity principle
  - Unit conversions

  - Applications to practical measurements

#### Cycle 6 — Day 17 — Wednesday

- **Domain:** Quantum
  - **Theme:** Differential Equations for Quantum Systems
- **Primary Topic:** ODE/PDE Foundations - Separation of Variables & Series Solutions
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - First-order linear ODEs: separation of variables, integrating factors
  - Second-order linear ODEs: homogeneous and non-homogeneous
  - Characteristic equations and roots
  - Wronskian and linear independence
  - Variation of parameters method
  - Series solutions: Frobenius method
  - Bessel and Legendre equations (introduction)
  - Partial differential equations basics
  - Separation of variables for PDEs
  - Boundary value problems
  - Sturm-Liouville theory (introduction)
  - Cross-Link (ECE): RLC circuit differential equations
  - Cross-Link (VHDL): Numerical ODE solvers in hardware
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Real-time differential equation solving
  - Cross-Link (Python): SciPy ODE integration
- **Learning Objective:** Build mathematical tools to solve ODE/PDEs used in quantum mechanics.
- **Session Breakdown:** 60m Theory / 30m Intuition / 40m Problem Solving / 20m Review (Total: 150m)
- **Deliverable:** Set of 5 Solved Problems (ODE solutions, series expansions, boundary value problems, PDE separation)
- **Tags:** #theory #practice #differential_equations #quantum

### Cycle 7: Vector Algebra & VHDL Concurrency (Days 22–28)

#### Cycle 7 — Day 22 — Monday

- **Domain:** ECE

- **Primary Topic:** UNIT VII: Vector Algebra - Vectors, Dot Product, Cross Product, Applications
- **Subtopics to cover:**

  - Vector addition and subtraction (parallelogram and triangle law)
  - Scalar multiplication and unit vectors

  - Triple scalar and triple vector products
  - Vector equations of lines and planes

  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Vector state representations

  - Wait statements: until, for, on, timeout
  - Process sensitivity and clocking
  - Delta cycle and simulation time
  - Race conditions and hazards
  - Proper synchronization techniques
  - Clock domain crossing basics
  - Metastability and synchronizers
  - Synthesis implications of concurrency
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Gate timing and race hazards
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): State synchronization
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Task scheduling

#### Cycle 7 — Day 24 — Wednesday

#### Cycle 7 — Day 25 — Thursday

- **Domain:** Embedded
  - **Theme:** Arduino Board Families & Architectural Differences

  - Synchronization delay and settling time
  - Mean time between failures (MTBF) analysis
  - Clock domain crossing hazards and solutions
  - Handshake protocols for reliable CDC
  - Gray code counters for safe multi-bit transfer
  - Pulse synchronizers and edge detectors
  - FIFO design across clock domains
  - CDC verification and simulation techniques

  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Quantum decoherence analogy to metastability

### Cycle 29: Advanced VHDL to Multi-Electron Atoms (Days 176–182)

#### Cycle 29 — Day 176 — Monday

- **Domain:** VHDL
  - **Theme:** Advanced State Machines & Datapath Design
- **Primary Topic:** VHDL State Machine Design Patterns - Moore and Mealy Architectures
- **Subtopics to cover:**
  - Finite state machine (FSM) fundamentals
  - Moore machines: outputs dependent on current state only
  - Mealy machines: outputs dependent on state and input
  - State encoding: binary, Gray code, one-hot, Johnson
  - FSM design methodology: state diagrams, state transition tables
  - VHDL encoding: process structures, next state logic, output logic
  - State explosion and hierarchical FSMs
  - Registered vs combinational outputs
  - FSM optimization: minimization, redundant state removal
  - Testbench design for FSM verification
  - Cross-Link (ECE): Datapath-control architecture in digital systems
  - Cross-Link (Quantum): Quantum state transitions as FSM
  - Cross-Link (Embedded): Protocol state machines in firmware
  - Cross-Link (Python): FSM simulation and visualization tools
- **Learning Objective:** Design efficient state machines using Moore/Mealy architectures with proper optimization and verification.
- **Session Breakdown:** 40m Theory / 30m Intuition / 50m HDL Coding / 30m Simulation (Total: 150m)
